Each task provides a locked data-preparation and evaluation script together with a baseline training script; the agent may only modify the training code, has no access to pretrained weights (with one controlled exception for semantic segmentation), no internet access, and must complete each task within a task-specific wall-clock budget (40-120 minutes) on a single GPU. We evaluate seven coding agents: five proprietary (Claude Code with Sonnet 4.6, Opus 4.6, and Opus 4.7; Codex CLI with GPT 5.5; and OpenCode with Qwen 3.6+) and two open-source (OpenCode with Kimi K2.5, Kimi K2.6). Across 5 runs per agent-task pair, we report substantial performance differences that reveal varying levels of implicit ML knowledge, planning ability, and time-budget management. The benchmark, harness, and all evaluation artifacts are publicly available on GitHub at https://github.com/Strolchii/1GC-7RC-Benchmark to facilitate reproducible comparison of future agents. Because our benchmark design is modular, the benchmark can be extended to new tasks and domains, adapted to different GPU budgets, and used to study multi-agent settings, making it a flexible platform for future research on autonomous research agents.

### [253] [Scale Determines Whether Language Models Organize Representation Geometry for Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17084)
*Weilun Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出子空间PGA指标，发现语言模型中间层的表示几何与预测输出对齐，但小模型在训练后期会失去这种对齐（尽管损失仍在下降），而大模型能保持对齐；这种差异源于少数主导方向迁移，掩盖而非破坏了底层的预测结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具仅刻画表示空间的几何形状，但没有探究这种形状是为何种目的而组织的。本文旨在回答：语言模型中间层的距离结构是否服务于预测任务（即与未嵌入矩阵的读出子空间对齐）？

Method: 提出Subspace PGA指标，通过比较层内距离结构与$W_U$读出子空间的对齐程度与随机子空间的对齐程度，衡量表示几何是否为预测而组织。在7个Pythia模型（70M-6.9B）和3个跨族模型上进行分析。

Result: 中间层几何显著为预测组织（峰值z=9-24），但存在尺度依赖：小模型（d≤1024）在训练后期逐渐失去对齐（即使损失持续下降），大模型（d≥2048）保持对齐。原因是少数主导方向从读出子空间迁移，掩盖了底层结构，移除后可恢复对齐。

Conclusion: 模型规模不仅决定预测性能，还决定表示几何的组织方式。谱指标和损失曲线无法捕捉这一关键区别。

Abstract: In language models, what a representation encodes is determined by the geometry of its representation space: distances, not activations, carry meaning. Existing tools characterize the shape of this geometry but do not ask what that shape is organized for. We introduce Subspace PGA, a metric that tests whether a layer's distance structure aligns with the readout subspace of the unembedding matrix $W_U$ more than with random subspaces of equal size. Across seven Pythia models (70M--6.9B) and three cross-family models, intermediate geometry is significantly organized for prediction (peak $z = 9$--$24$), but the degree is scale-dependent: small models ($d \leq 1024$) progressively lose it at late layers during training -- even as loss keeps improving -- while large models ($d \geq 2048$) preserve it throughout. We trace this to a capacity trade-off: a few dominant directions migrate away from $W_U$'s readout, masking rather than destroying the predictive structure beneath, and removing them restores alignment. Neither spectral metrics nor loss curves capture this distinction. Scale thus determines not only how well a model predicts, but how its representation geometry is organized to do so.

### [254] [OpenJarvis: Personal AI, On Personal Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17172)
*Jon Saad-Falcon,Avanika Narayan,Robby Manihani,Tanvir Bhathal,Herumb Shandilya,Hakki Orhun Akengin,Gabriel Bo,Andrew Park,Matthew Hart,Caia Costello,Chuan Li,Christopher Ré,Azalia Mirhoseini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出OpenJarvis架构，通过分解个人AI栈为五个独立基元（智能、引擎、Agent、工具与记忆、学习），并引入LLM引导的规范搜索，在推理时完全本地运行，缩小本地模型与云端模型的性能差距（平均仅差3.2个百分点），同时降低约800倍API成本和4倍延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有个人AI栈（如OpenClaw、Hermes Agent）几乎将所有查询路由到云端前沿模型，频繁暴露敏感本地数据；直接用本地模型替换云端模型会导致准确率大幅下降（25-39个百分点）；现有优化手段仅能调整提示词，最多缩小5个百分点的差距，无法解决根本问题。

Method: 提出OpenJarvis架构：(1) 将个人AI系统抽象为五个独立基元（Intelligence、Engine、Agents、Tools & Memory、Learning）的 typed spec；(2) 引入LLM引导的规范搜索（LLM-guided spec search），在搜索时由云端前沿模型提议编辑，仅接受非回归编辑，最终生成的spec在推理时完全本地运行。

Result: 在8个基准测试中的4个上，本地spec匹配或超过云端准确率；平均仅落后最佳云端基线3.2个百分点；边际API成本降低约800倍；端到端延迟降低4倍。

Conclusion: OpenJarvis证明通过解耦个人AI栈的各个基元并进行联合优化，可以大幅缩小本地与云端模型之间的性能差距，同时保留本地模型的隐私和低成本优势。

Abstract: Personal AI stacks, like OpenClaw and Hermes Agent, are becoming central to daily work, yet they route nearly every query (often over sensitive local data) to cloud-hosted frontier models. Replacing frontier models with local models inside existing stacks does not work: swapping Claude Opus 4.6 for Qwen3.5-9B drops accuracy by 25-39 pp across personal AI tasks like PinchBench and GAIA. Existing stacks bundle agentic prompts, tool descriptions, memory configuration, and runtime settings around a specific cloud model. Only the prompts can be tuned, and state-of-the-art prompt optimizers close just 5 pp of the local-cloud gap on their own. This motivates a decomposed personal AI stack: one that exposes individual primitives which can be optimized individually or jointly to close the local-cloud gap. We present OpenJarvis, an architecture that represents a personal AI system as a typed spec over five primitives: Intelligence, Engine, Agents, Tools & Memory, and Learning. Each primitive is an independently editable field, making the stack end-to-end optimizable and measurable against accuracy, cost, and latency. Towards closing the local-cloud gap without surrendering local-model properties, OpenJarvis introduces LLM-guided spec search, a local-cloud collaboration in which frontier cloud models propose edits across the spec at search time, only non-regressing edits are accepted, and the resulting spec runs entirely on-device at inference time. With LLM-guided spec search, on-device specs match or exceed cloud accuracy on 4 of 8 benchmarks and land within 3.2 pp of the best cloud baseline on average. They also reduce marginal API cost by ~800x and end-to-end latency by 4x.

</details>


### [255] [FishBack: Pullback Fisher Geometry for Optimal Activation Steering in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17231)
*Sihan Wang,Jiayi Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 FishBack 框架，发现语言模型的激活空间并非欧几里得，而是由 Fisher 信息度量主导。基于此推导出闭式最优转向方向，在 GPT-2 上相比现有方法（CAA、ActAdd、ITI 等）显著降低离目标 KL 散度 1.3-2.5 倍，并统一解释了各方法的性能差异源于其隐式度量的谱成本比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有激活转向方法都假设语言模型的激活空间是欧几里得空间，但这一假设在实际中并不成立。作者想从信息几何角度揭示真实几何结构，并据此设计更优的转向方法。

Method: 1. 利用 softmax 层的 Fisher 信息度量，通过后续层的 Jacobian 拉回至中间层激活空间，定义非欧几何结构。2. 推导出闭式最优转向方向（pullback steering），无需数据驱动的几何估计或流形拟合。3. 提出 FishBack 框架，支持逐层递归分解，统一解释现有方法（CAA、ActAdd、ITI 等）隐式使用的近似度量。

Result: 1. GPT-2 上相对谱范数偏差超过 97%，有效维度仅占环境的 2-17%。2. FishBack 在三个动词形态概念和四个层上均优于所有欧几里得基线，离目标 KL 降低 1.3-2.5 倍（相比欧几里得梯度上升），1.5 倍（相比 CAA，在匹配概念概率下）。3. 各方法的性能差距可以通过单一谱诊断（隐式度量成本与 Fisher 最优成本之比）定量预测。

Conclusion: 语言模型的激活空间本质上是非欧几何的，Fisher 信息度量提供了更准确的描述。FishBack 框架不仅在实践中效果更好，还统一了现有方法的理论理解，指出了它们性能差异的根源。

Abstract: Activation steering methods modify intermediate representations of language models to control output behavior, but universally assume the activation space is Euclidean. We show this assumption fails drastically: the local geometry induced by the model's own output behavior -- the Fisher information metric of the softmax layer, pulled back through the Jacobian of subsequent layers -- deviates from the Euclidean metric by over 97% in relative spectral norm on GPT-2, with an effective dimensionality of only 2--17% of the ambient space. From this pullback Fisher metric, we derive a closed-form steering equation that identifies the minimum-distortion direction for any target concept, yielding a closed-form optimal direction at each point that can be applied iteratively without manifold fitting or data-driven geometry estimation. We call the resulting framework FishBack. The metric admits a layer-wise recursive decomposition, which reveals that existing methods -- CAA, ActAdd, ITI, and others -- each implicitly adopt a particular approximate metric, and that their performance gaps are quantitatively predicted by a single spectral diagnostic: the ratio of their implicit metric's cost to the Fisher-optimal cost. On GPT-2, iterative pullback steering consistently outperforms all Euclidean baselines across three verb-morphology concepts and four layers, with off-target KL reductions of $1.3\times$--$2.5\times$ relative to Euclidean gradient ascent and $1.5\times$ relative to CAA at matched concept probability.

</details>


### [256] [DISA: Offline Importance Sampling for Distribution-Matching LLM-RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17295)
*Shaobo Wang,Yujie Chen,Yafeng Sun,Wenjie Qiu,Zhihui Xie,Sihang Li,Yucheng Li,Huiqiang Jiang,Xingzhang Ren,Xuming Hu,Dayiheng Liu,Linfeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DISA将分布匹配强化学习中的配分函数估计从策略优化循环中解耦出来，通过离线采样和重要性采样估计配分函数，从而避免校准误差扭曲策略更新，在数学和代码基准上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分布匹配RL方法在策略学习的同时在线学习配分函数，导致配分函数的校准误差会直接扭曲策略更新且无法独立诊断，需要将二者解耦。

Method: DISA：先离线采样轨迹，通过重要性采样估计配分函数，冻结该估计值后再进行策略优化，从而将配分函数估计与策略学习在数据、梯度、损失和诊断上完全分离。

Result: 在6个数学和3个代码基准上，DISA匹配或超越在线耦合基线FlowRL，优于奖励最大化基线GRPO和GSPO，相比LoRASFT蒸馏在Mean@8上提升高达13.8分，且保留更多策略级多样性。

Conclusion: 配分函数与策略优化的解耦是可行的，且能提升分布匹配RL的性能、可诊断性和多样性，敏感度分析符合理论预期的偏差-方差模式。

Abstract: Modern reasoning agents are increasingly evaluated on their ability to generate multiple valid solution paths, plans, or tool-use traces for a given input. Standard reward-maximizing RL tends to collapse onto the most easily reinforced high-reward mode, whereas distribution-matching RL aims to allocate probability mass across the entire reward-shaped solution set. Achieving this objective requires computing a prompt-dependent partition function over the trajectory space. Because existing distribution-matching methods learn this partition function online alongside the policy, calibration errors in the partition function directly distort policy updates and remain impossible to diagnose independently. We introduce DISA, short for Decoupled Importance-Sampled Anchoring, which moves this calibration problem outside the RL loop. DISA draws proposal trajectories offline, estimates the partition function via importance sampling, and freezes the resulting partition-function estimate before policy optimization begins. This decoupling preserves the distribution-matching objective while strictly separating partition-function estimation from policy learning in data, gradients, loss, and diagnostics. Empirically, on two open-weight backbones across six math and three code benchmarks, DISA matches or exceeds the online-coupled distribution-matching baseline FlowRL, outperforms rewardmaximization baselines GRPO and GSPO on math averages, and exceeds LoRASFT distillation by up to 13.8 Mean@8 points on the same offline trajectories. An LLM-as-judge evaluation further shows that DISA retains substantially more strategy-level diversity than reward-maximization baselines, and sensitivity studies on the proposal strength and inverse temperature follow the bias-variance pattern predicted by the analysis.

</details>


### [257] [Compress the Context, Keep the Commitments: A Formal Framework for Verifiable LLM Context Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17304)
*Natalia Trukhina,Vadim Vashkelis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Context Codec，一个基于承诺（commitment）级别的对话上下文压缩框架，将对话状态表示为类型化、有来源的语义原子，并定义提取、归一化、表示、渲染、验证五个环节，以及关键原子召回率等评估指标，使上下文压缩变得可验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有上下文管理方法（截断、检索、摘要、记忆系统、token级压缩）很少明确指定哪些语义承诺必须在压缩后保留，以及如何衡量保留效果。

Method: 提出 Context Codec 框架：1) 将对话状态表示为带类型、来源、身份、等价关系、冲突、置信度、风险等级的语义原子；2) 分离提取、归一化、表示、渲染、验证五个环节；3) 定义关键原子召回率、加权原子召回率、承诺密度、往返可恢复性等指标；4) 提出语义压缩错误分类法、归一化流程、低置信度与安全关键原子的保守回退规则；5) 设计 Context Compression Language (CCL) 紧凑表示格式。

Result: 诊断研究表明 CCL-Core 在结构化文本与 JSON 之间占据了有用中间地带：比文本更显式可审计，通常比 JSON 更紧凑，且比高度压缩符号风险更低。

Conclusion: 本文并非主张某种速记法能解决压缩问题，而是提供一个使上下文压缩可验证的框架：压缩对话，保留承诺。

Abstract: LLM context is not just tokens; it is a set of commitments. Long-running conversations accumulate goals, constraints, decisions, preferences, tool results, retrieved evidence, artifacts, and safety boundaries that future responses must preserve. Existing context-management methods reduce length through truncation, retrieval, summarization, memory systems, or token-level prompt compression, but they rarely specify which semantic commitments must survive compression or how their preservation should be measured. We propose Context Codec, a commitment-level framework for compressing prompts and chat histories.
  Context Codec represents dialogue state as typed, source-grounded semantic atoms with canonical identity, equivalence, conflict, confidence, risk, and evidence spans. It separates five concerns - extraction, normalization, representation, rendering, and verification - and introduces metrics for Critical Atom Recall, Weighted Atom Recall, Commitment Density, and round-trip recoverability. It also defines a taxonomy of semantic compression errors, a concrete normalization procedure, conservative fallback rules for low-confidence and safety-critical atoms, and Context Compression Language (CCL), an ASCII-first compact rendering of canonical JSON atoms. In a small diagnostic study, CCL-Core occupies a useful middle ground between structured prose and JSON: more explicit and auditable than prose, usually more compact than JSON, and less risky than heavily minified notation. The result is not a claim that shorthand solves compression, but a framework for making context compression verifiable: compress the conversation, keep the commitments.

### [258] [CasualSynth: Generating Structurally Sound Synthetic Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17528)
*Zehua Cheng,Wei Dai,Jiahao Sun,Thomas Lukasiewicz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出CausalSynth框架，通过解耦因果结构生成与语义实现，利用结构因果模型生成符合因果关系的"骨架"，再由大语言模型约束性地转化为高维观测数据（如临床笔记），并通过迭代一致性验证模块闭环修正，解决了LLM在合成数据中覆盖预设因果事实的"语义后门"问题。在三个因果基准上，该框架能保持条件独立性（假阳性率接近α=0.05），实现率超96%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型能生成逼真的合成数据，但无法保证其输出尊重目标领域的因果机制。现有方法缺乏对合成数据因果有效性的保障，因此需要一个能同时确保因果有效性和语义丰富性的框架。

Method: 三阶段框架：(1) SCM通过DAG上的结构方程结合祖先采样生成因果骨架；(2) LLM作为受约束的"实现器"，将骨架映射为高维观测；(3) 迭代一致性验证模块通过确定性提取检测结构违规并反馈给LLM形成闭环修正。此外，提出了"语义后门"问题并通过迭代机制减少选择偏差。

Result: 在ASIA、ALARM和MIMIC-Struct三个因果基准上，CausalSynth的假阳性率接近名义水平α=0.05，使用70B参数LLM时实现率达96%以上，并支持原则性的干预和反事实生成。

Conclusion: CausalSynth有效解耦了因果结构生成与语义实现，通过闭环修正机制克服了LLM的"语义后门"问题，生成的合成数据既满足因果有效性又具备语义丰富性，为因果引导的合成数据生成提供了可靠框架。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) generate realistic synthetic data but offer no guarantee that their outputs respect the causal mechanisms governing the target domain. We introduce CausalSynth, a framework that decouples causal structure generation from semantic realization, yielding synthetic data that is both causally valid and linguistically rich. The framework operates in three phases. First, a Structural Causal Model (SCM) - a tuple of structural equations defined over a directed acyclic graph (DAG) generates causal skeletons, i.e., variable assignments that satisfy the Global Markov Property of the governing DAG, via ancestral sampling. Second, an LLM acts as a constrained \emph{realizer}, a conditional translator that maps each skeleton to a high-dimensional observation such as a clinical note or a transaction log. Third, an Iterative Consistency Verification module detects structural violations through deterministic extraction and feeds targeted corrections back to the LLM, forming a closed-loop refinement process. We identify the Semantic Backdoor problem the systematic tendency of LLMs to override imposed causal facts with pre-training priors -- and prove that our iterative mechanism reduces the resulting selection bias relative to standard rejection sampling. On three causal benchmarks (ASIA, ALARM, and MIMIC-Struct), CausalSynth preserved conditional independencies with false-positive rates near the nominal $α=0.05$ level and achieved realizability rates above 96% with 70B-parameter LLM backbones. The framework additionally supports principled interventional and counterfactual generation through noise retention and graph mutilation.

*Minghao Tian,Yunfei Xie,Chen Wei*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准GRPO采用近策略训练，系统开销大。作者探究GRPO能容忍多大程度的离线（off-policy）训练，以减少频繁的rollout-优化切换开销。

Method: 将训练组织为少量（如4个）大序列生成-优化阶段，引入高rollout陈旧性；结合松弛裁剪（保留有用陈旧梯度）和负优势否决（移除不稳定更新）来稳定训练。

Result: 在5种语言模型和多个数学推理基准上，Mu-GRPO匹配或超越标准GRPO性能，并实现约2倍的实际训练时间加速。

Abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has been a key driver of recent progress in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models, but it is typically trained in a low-staleness, near-on-policy regime that incurs substantial system overhead. We ask a simple question: How off-policy can GRPO be? We show that GRPO-style algorithms can tolerate substantially larger rollout staleness than previously assumed, and propose Mu-GRPO, an RL training framework that organizes training into a small number (e.g., four) of large sequential generation-optimization stages. This design induces high rollout staleness while greatly reducing rollout-optimization switching overhead. To stabilize learning under stale data, Mu-GRPO combines relaxed clipping, which preserves useful stale-rollout gradients, with negative-advantage veto, which removes destabilizing post-trigger suffix updates in negative-advantage responses. Across five language models and multiple math reasoning benchmarks, Mu-GRPO matches or exceeds the performance of standard GRPO while achieving around 2x speedup in wall-clock training time, establishing a substantially improved performance-efficiency trade-off for LLM reinforcement learning.

### [260] [HINT-SD: Targeted Hindsight Self-Distillation for Long-Horizon Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17873)
*Woongyeng Yeo,Yumin Choi,Taekyung Ki,Sung Ju Hwang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出HINT-SD框架，通过全轨迹事后视角选择失败相关动作，仅对目标动作跨度进行反馈条件蒸馏，在长程LLM智能体训练中提升效果并降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏结果奖励无法识别导致失败的具体中间动作，而现有每轮生成反馈的方法在多数成功/中性回合中效率低下，且固定轮次反馈常监督不到实际导致失败的动作。

Method: HINT-SD：利用完整轨迹的事后回溯（hindsight）选择与失败相关的动作跨度，仅对这些目标动作应用反馈条件蒸馏（feedback-conditioned distillation），跳过无关回合的反馈生成。

Result: 在BFCL v3和AppWorld上，相比密集每轮反馈基线，性能提升高达18.80%，同时每个训练步骤的时间降低了2.26倍。

Abstract: Training long-horizon LLM agents with reinforcement learning is challenging because sparse outcome rewards reveal whether a task succeeds, but not which intermediate actions caused the outcome or how they should be corrected. Recent methods alleviate this issue by generating rewards or textual hints from turn-level action-output signals, or by using feedback-conditioned self-distillation. However, generating feedback at every turn is inefficient when many intermediate turns are already successful or neutral, and applying feedback at a fixed or misaligned turn often fails to supervise the actions that contributed to the failure. To bridge this gap, we propose HINT-SD, a targeted self-distillation framework that uses full-trajectory hindsight to select failure-relevant actions and applies feedback-conditioned distillation only on targeted action spans. Experiments on BFCL v3 and AppWorld show that our method improves over the dense per-turn feedback baseline by up to 18.80 percent while achieving 2.26$\times$ lower time per training step, suggesting that selecting where to distill is a key factor for both effective and efficient long-horizon agent training.

Abstract: We study KV cache eviction under a shared globally capped decode-time harness. Faithful Ada-KV/QUEST add ${\sim}0.03$--$0.04$ F1 on Mistral-7B and Phi-3.5 beyond simplified variants. A NIAH-32K regime-transfer pilot on Qwen3-4B (decode vs.\ prefill, $C{\in}\{512,2048\}$) shows near-identical protection lifts (ratio 0.99--1.00). At 64K, protection helps but recovery is modest; faithful per-head scoring matches full-cache ceiling on Gemma-3-4B at 6.3\% retention only when the model already supports strong 64K retrieval without eviction. Overall: protection dominates; scoring differences are secondary once boundaries are guarded; per-head allocation gives a further modest gain.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Existing expressivity results for transformers typically rely on hardmax attention, high precision, and other architectural modifications that disconnect them from the models used in practice. We bridge this gap by analyzing standard transformer decoders with softmax attention and rounding of activations and attention weights, while allowing depth and width to grow logarithmically with the context length. As an intermediate step, we construct hardmax transformers with ternary activations and well-separated attention scores that simulate Turing machines using Chain-of-Thought (CoT). This lets us convert the constructions to equivalent softmax transformers without the unrealistic parameter magnitudes or activation precision that prior approaches would require. Using the same technique, we analyze a recently proposed summarized CoT paradigm and show that it simulates Turing machines more efficiently, with model size scaling logarithmically in a space bound rather than a time bound. We empirically test predictions made by our results on a Sudoku reasoning task and find better alignment with learnability than for prior high-precision results. Our code is available at https://github.com/moritzbroe/transformer-expressivity.

*Peilin Wu,Xinlu Zhang,Kun Wan,Wentian Zhao,Gang Wu,Xinya Du,Zhiyu Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AMARIS 通过引入持久化评估记忆机制，将基于 rubrics 的奖励塑形从无状态的逐步骤启发式方法转变为证据驱动的闭环，在强化学习微调 LLMs 中持续积累历史评估知识以动态调整 rubrics，在封闭和开放域任务中显著优于基线，且异步执行仅带来约 5% 的时间开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于 rubrics 的奖励塑形方法虽然引入了多维奖励信号，但仅在当前步骤或局部对比后即丢弃评估结果，无法长期积累和复用评估知识，导致系统需从头推导评估原则，难以检测重复出现的次优行为，也缺乏训练历史驱动的课程式学习过程。

Method: AMARIS 在每步训练中分析单个 rollout，聚合为步骤级摘要，通过静态检索（最近步骤）和动态检索（语义匹配）从持久化评估记忆中获取历史上下文，基于累积分析更新 rubrics。该过程异步运行于 RL 主循环外，最小化开销。

Result: 在封闭域和开放域任务中，AMARIS 持续优于基线方法。消融实验表明静态和动态记忆检索均贡献性能增益，二者结合效果最佳；适中的检索预算即可获得大部分增益；异步执行仅增加约 5% 的时间开销。

Conclusion: 持久化评估记忆能够将基于 rubrics 的奖励塑形从无状态的逐步骤启发式方法转变为证据驱动的迭代闭环，有效提升 LLM 强化学习微调效果。

Abstract: Rubric-based reward shaping is an effective method for fine-tuning LLMs via RL, where structured rubrics decompose standard outcome rewards into multiple dimensions to provide richer reward signals. Recent works make the rubrics adaptive based on local signals such as the rollouts from the current step or pairwise comparisons. However, these methods discard the diagnostics produced during evaluation after immediate use and prevent the long-term accumulation and strategic reuse of evaluation knowledge. This forces the system to re-derive evaluation principles from scratch, limits its ability to detect recurring suboptimal behaviors, and forfeits the curriculum-like progression that a persistent training history would naturally support. To address these limitations, we introduce AMARIS, which grounds rubric modifications in long-term training history. At each training step, AMARIS analyzes individual rollouts, aggregates findings into step-level summaries, retrieves relevant historical context from a persistent evaluation memory through both static (recent steps) and dynamic (semantically matched) retrieval, and updates rubrics based on these accumulated analyses. This procedure runs asynchronously alongside the normal RL loop with minimal overhead. Experiments across both closed and open-ended domains show that AMARIS consistently outperforms the baselines. Ablation studies show that static and dynamic memory retrieval contributes to the performance gain and their combination provides the strongest results with moderate retrieval budgets sufficient to provide most of the gain, and that the entire pipeline adds only ~5\% time overhead through asynchronous execution. These results show that persistent evaluation memory can transform rubric-based reward shaping from a stateless, per-step heuristic into an evidence-driven loop for RL training.

</details>


### [264] [Post-Trained MoE Can Skip Half Experts via Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18643)
*Xingtai Lv,Li Sheng,Kaiyan Zhang,Yichen You,Siyan Gao,Xueheng Luo,Yuxin Zuo,Yuchen Fan,Junlin Yang,Ganqu Cui,Bingning Wang,Fan Yang,Youbang Sun,Ning Ding,Bowen Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ZEDA是一种低成本框架，通过注入零输出专家和两阶段自蒸馏，将预训练的静态MoE模型转化为动态MoE，在不显著损失精度的情况下消除50%以上的专家FLOPs，并实现约1.20倍的推理加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态MoE方法通常需要从头预训练或任务特定微调，缺乏将已训练好的静态MoE模型高效转化为动态MoE的方案，而后者能通过让简单token跳过不必要的专家来直接降低推理成本。

Method: ZEDA框架包含两个核心：1）在每个MoE层注入无参数的零输出专家以稳定架构转换；2）通过两阶段自蒸馏进行适配，以原始MoE为冻结教师，并应用组级平衡损失。

Result: 在Qwen3-30B-A3B和GLM-4.7-Flash上，覆盖11个数学、代码和指令跟随基准测试，消除50%以上专家FLOPs且精度损失极小；比最强动态MoE基线高出6.1和4.0个百分点；实现约1.20倍端到端推理加速。

Conclusion: ZEDA有效实现了从静态MoE到动态MoE的低成本转化，显著降低推理计算量，同时保持模型性能，为已训练MoE模型的高效部署提供了实用方案。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) scales language models efficiently through sparse expert activation, and its dynamic variant further reduces computation by adjusting the activated experts in an input-dependent manner. Existing dynamic MoE methods usually rely on pre-training from scratch or task-specific adaptation, leaving the practical conversion of fully trained MoE underexplored. Enabling such adaptation would directly alleviate the inference costs by allowing easy tokens to bypass unnecessary expert during serving. This paper introduces Zero-Expert Self-Distillation Adaptation (ZEDA), a low-cost framework that transforms post-trained static MoE models into efficient dynamic ones. To stabilize this architectural conversion, ZEDA injects parameter-free zero-output experts into each MoE layer and adapts the augmented model through two-stage self-distillation, utilizing the original MoE as a frozen teacher and applying a group-level balancing loss. On Qwen3-30B-A3B and GLM-4.7-Flash across 11 benchmarks spanning math, code, and instruction following, ZEDA eliminates over 50% of expert FLOPs at marginal accuracy loss. It outperforms the strongest dynamic MoE baseline by 6.1 and 4.0 points on the two models, and delivers ~1.20$\times$ end-to-end inference speedup.

</details>


### [265] [An Assessment of Human vs. Model Uncertainty in Soft-Label Learning and Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18648)
*Maja Pavlovic,Silviu Paun,Massimo Poesio*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过控制实验，将人类软标签带来的准确率提升与数据修正效应分离，发现人类软标签的主要价值在于作为正则化器，提升模型在困难样本上的校准度和训练稳定性，而非单纯的准确率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究将人类软标签的优势（校准能力）与隐式的错误数据修正（模式偏移）混为一谈，无法区分软标签的真实效果。需要解耦这两者，以厘清人类软标签的独特价值。

Method: 在MNIST及其合成变体上，对子集进行重新标注以提取人类不确定性；通过控制实验将软标签监督与底层标签模式偏移解耦，对比人类软标签与合成标签的训练效果。

Result: 人类软标签虽能带来准确率提升，但更重要的价值在于：1) 作为正则化器改善困难样本的模型校准度；2) 促进跨训练轮次的稳定收敛。数据集制图显示，人类软标签训练的模型能反映人类不确定性，而合成标签则不能。

Conclusion: 本文为人类-AI不确定性对齐提供了诊断性测试平台，揭示了人类软标签的核心价值在于校准与稳定性，而非简单的准确率提升。

Abstract: Central to human-aligned AI is understanding the benefits of human-elicited labels over synthetic alternatives. While human soft-labels improve calibration by capturing uncertainty, prior studies conflate these benefits with the implicit correction of mislabeled data (mode shifts), obscuring true effects of soft-labels. We present a controlled audit of soft-label learning across MNIST and a synthetic variant, re-annotating subsets to extract human uncertainty. By decoupling soft-label supervision from underlying label mode shifts, we show that while human soft-labels do provide accuracy gains, their larger value lies in acting as a regularizer that improves model calibration on difficult samples and promotes stable convergence across training runs. Dataset cartography reveals models trained on human soft-labels mirror human uncertainty, whereas those trained on synthetic labels fail to align with humans. Broadly, this work provides a diagnostic testbed for human-AI uncertainty alignment.

</details>


### [266] [General Preference Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18721)
*Muhammad Umer,Muhammad Ahmed Mohsin,Ahsan Bilal,Arslan Chaudhry,Andreas Haupt,Sanmi Koyejo,Emily Fox,John M. Cioffi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了通用偏好强化学习（GPRL），通过将偏好建模为多维结构而非标量，在开放任务上实现了比现有方法更强的对齐效果，同时有效抵抗奖励作弊。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型对齐方法存在两难：在线RL（如PPO）依赖可编程验证器，只能用于数学/代码；偏好优化（如DPO）虽处理开放任务但缺乏持续探索。根本问题在于标量奖励模型无法捕捉质量的多维性，容易导致RL在单一维度上坍塌。

Method: 基于通用偏好模型（GPM）将响应嵌入k个斜对称子空间，GPRL在策略更新时：1）计算每维的组相对优势并独立归一化；2）用上下文相关特征值聚合；3）通过闭环漂移监控器检测单轴利用，实时重加权维度和收紧信任域。

Result: 在Llama-3-8B-Instruct上，AlpacaEval 2.0达到56.51%的LC胜率，在Arena-Hard、MT-Bench、WildBench上优于SimPO和SPPO，且能抵抗长期训练中的奖励作弊。

Conclusion: 多维偏好建模结合结构化策略更新，是弥合在线RL与偏好优化之间鸿沟的有效方案，为开放任务对齐提供了新范式。

Abstract: Post-training has split large language model (LLM) alignment into two largely disconnected tracks. Online reinforcement learning (RL) with verifiable rewards drives emergent reasoning on math and code but depends on a programmatic verifier that cannot reach open-ended tasks, while preference optimization handles open-ended generation yet forgoes the continuous exploration that powers online RL. Closing this gap requires a verifier for open-ended quality, but a scalar reward model is the wrong shape for the job. Quality is multi-dimensional, and any scalar score is an incomplete proxy that lets online RL collapse onto whichever axis the score is most sensitive to. We turn instead to the General Preference Model (GPM), which embeds responses into $k$ skew-symmetric subspaces and represents preference as a structured, intransitivity-aware comparison. Building on this, we propose General Preference Reinforcement Learning (GPRL), which carries the $k$-way structure through to the policy update. GPRL computes per-dimension group-relative advantages, normalizes each on its own scale so no axis can dominate, and aggregates them with context-dependent eigenvalues. The same structure powers a closed-loop drift monitor that detects single-axis exploitation and corrects it on the fly by reweighting dimensions and tightening the trust region. Starting from $\texttt{Llama-3-8B-Instruct}$, GPRL reaches a length-controlled win rate of $56.51\%$ on AlpacaEval~2.0 while also outperforming SimPO and SPPO on Arena-Hard, MT-Bench, and WildBench by resisting reward hacking across extended training runs.

</details>

### [267] [NeuroMAS: Multi-Agent Systems as Neural Networks with Joint Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16757)
*Haoran Lu,Luyang Fang,Wenxuan Zhong,Ping Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出NeuroMAS方法，将多智能体语言系统设计为可训练、可扩展的类神经网络架构，通过强化学习训练智能体间的通信与协作，取代传统手工设计的工作流方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体系统通常依赖手工设计的工作流（预设角色与通信协议），缺乏可训练性和可扩展性，限制了系统能力的规模化发展。

Method: 将多智能体系统视为类神经网络架构：LLM智能体作为节点，文本信号作为边；智能体无预设角色但具有结构感知能力；通过强化学习训练节点间的通信、专业化和协调方式。

Result: NeuroMAS在推理时和训练后的多智能体基线上均显著提升；系统规模扩展存在路径依赖——从零训练大系统困难，但从已训练的小系统逐步增长则可行。

Conclusion: 学习型神经多智能体系统为LLMs提供了一种有前景的规模化扩展方向，将多智能体设计从工作流工程转向架构设计。

Abstract: Multi-agent language systems are often built as hand-designed workflows, where agents are assigned semantic roles and communication protocols are specified in advance. We propose NeuroMAS, a method that first treats a multi-agent language system as a trainable and scalable neural-network-like architecture with LLM agents as nodes and intermediate textual signals as edges. In NeuroMAS, agent nodes are role-free but structure-aware: the topology only determines how information can flow in general, while reinforcement learning training determines how nodes communicate, specialize, and coordinate. This formulation shifts multi-agent design from workflow engineering toward architecture design, where depth, width, connectivity, and growth protocol become scalable sources of capability. Further, we provide a theoretical perspective showing why such modular textual computation is more parameter-efficient when tasks admit hierarchical decompositions. Experiments show that NeuroMAS improves significantly over both inference-time and trained multi-agent baselines. We further find that organizational scaling is path-dependent: larger systems can be challenging to train from scratch, but become feasible when grown progressively from smaller trained systems. These results suggest that learned neural multi-agent systems are a promising scaling axis for LLMs.

</details>


### [268] [Reliability and Effectiveness of Autonomous AI Agents in Supply Chain Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17036)
*Carol Xuan Long,David Simchi-Levi,Feng Zhu,Huangyuan Su,Andre P. Calmon,Flavio P. Calmon*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文以MIT啤酒游戏为平台研究多层级供应链中的自主生成式AI智能体，发现模型能力是决定性因素，推理模型可超越人类表现并降低67%成本，但引入"智能体牛鞭效应"导致决策不可靠性沿供应链层级放大，并提出基于GRPO的强化学习后训练框架来提升可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对自主生成式AI智能体在多层级供应链中的系统评估，特别是其可靠性问题未被充分认识。作者希望通过揭示智能体牛鞭效应并寻找缓解方法，提升AI供应链管理的实际应用价值。

Method: 使用MIT啤酒游戏作为供应链仿真环境，识别四个推理时杠杆（模型选择、策略与护栏、集中式数据共享、提示工程），并开发GRPO强化学习后训练框架联合优化系统级供应链奖励。

Result: 1) 推理模型可超越人类表现，优化后成本降低67%；2) 发现智能体牛鞭效应——决策方差在设施间和同一设施内不同时间步上均会放大；3) 重复采样无法有效缓解此问题；4) GRPO后训练能显著减少尾部事件并抑制智能体牛鞭效应。

Conclusion: 自主AI智能体在供应链管理中潜力巨大但存在固有可靠性风险，智能体牛鞭效应是多智能体系统的内在特性，GRPO后训练是提升可靠性的有效途径。

Abstract: This paper studies autonomous generative AI agents in multi-echelon supply chains using the MIT Beer Game. We identify four inference-time levers that shape performance: model selection, policies and guardrails, centralized data sharing, and prompt engineering. Model capability is the dominant factor: an out-of-the-box reasoning model exceeds human-level performance, and optimized reasoning models reduce costs by up to 67% relative to human teams. However, strong average performance masks substantial reliability risks. We introduce the agent bullwhip effect, the amplification of decision unreliability across echelons, manifesting along two dimensions: decision variance increases both across facilities at the same point in time and within the same facility across time. We develop a mathematical framework showing that this phenomenon is inherent to multi-agent systems that involve coordination and information delays, and we demonstrate that repeated sampling fails to meaningfully reduce it. To address this limitation, we propose a Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)-based reinforcement-learning post-training framework that trains a shared base LLM using system-level supply-chain rewards. GRPO post-training substantially reduces tail events, curtails agent bullwhip, and improves the reliability of autonomous supply-chain agents.

### [270] [CAM-Bench: A Benchmark for Computational and Applied Mathematics in Lean](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17255)
*Wentao Long,Yunfei Zhang,Chenyi Li,Li Zhou,Chumin Sun,Zaiwen Wen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CAM-Bench是一个包含1,000个Lean 4定理证明目标的基准测试，专注于计算数学与应用数学领域（优化、数值线性代数、数值分析），通过依赖恢复流水线将教科书习题转化为形式化证明目标，并评估了现有大语言模型在该基准上的表现及失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有形式化定理证明基准主要聚焦于奥林匹克级问题和代数领域，计算数学与应用数学领域被严重忽视，缺乏相应的评估基准。

Method: 构建了一个依赖恢复流水线，从教科书习题中恢复局部定义的上下文（定义、符号、算法、基础结论），将问题标准化为独立非形式化定理，再翻译为Lean 4目标，并通过编译验证和语义审查双重校验。

Result: 发布了1,000个Lean 4定理证明目标，每个问题附带原始习题、恢复的上下文、标准化非形式化定理和最终Lean目标；评估了主流大语言模型和形式化智能体在该基准上的表现。

Conclusion: CAM-Bench填补了计算数学领域形式化定理证明基准的空白，揭示了现有模型在跟踪局部假设、应用基础结论、证明分解和长期推理控制方面的常见失败模式。

Abstract: Formal theorem-proving benchmarks enable mechanically verifiable evaluation of mathematical reasoning in large language models. However, existing benchmarks mainly focus on Olympiad-style problems and algebraic domains, leaving computational and applied mathematics underrepresented. We introduce CAM-Bench, a Lean 4 theorem-proving benchmark of 1,000 Lean proof targets in computational and applied mathematics, with coverage spanning optimization, numerical linear algebra, and numerical analysis. These problems are adapted from textbook exercises and often depend on locally introduced definitions, notation, algorithms, and elementary results. To construct CAM-Bench, we develop a dependency-recovery pipeline that reconstructs the local textbook context needed to state each problem faithfully. It then normalizes each problem into a standalone informal theorem and translates it into a Lean target. We validate the resulting formal problems through Lean compilation and semantic review, checking both formal correctness and semantic alignment with the original exercises. For each problem, we release the raw exercise, recovered context, normalized informal theorem, and final Lean target. CAM-Bench complements existing formal mathematics benchmarks by targeting applied mathematics problems that rely on textbook concepts and elementary theorems, many of which are not directly available as standard Mathlib4 lemmas. We evaluate widely used large language models and formalization agents on CAM-Bench, and analyze common failure modes in tracking local assumptions, applying elementary results, decomposing proofs, and maintaining long-horizon control in Lean.

### [271] [Unleashing LLMs in Bayesian Optimization: Preference-Guided Framework for Scientific Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17976)
*Xinzhe Yuan,Zhuo Chen,Jianshu Zhang,Huan Xiong,Nanyang Ye,Yuqiang Li,Qinying Gu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出LGBO框架，将大语言模型的语义推理持续集成到贝叶斯优化循环中，通过区域提升偏好机制显著加速科学实验优化，在多项基准测试和新湿实验（Fe-Cr电池电解液优化）中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统贝叶斯优化在冷启动阶段收敛慢、高维场景扩展性差，限制了其在真实科学问题中的应用。现有LLM方法仅用于预热初始化或候选生成，未能持续利用LLM的语义推理能力。

Method: 提出LGBO框架，核心创新是**区域提升偏好机制**，将LLM驱动的偏好嵌入到每一次迭代中，稳定可控地偏移代理模型均值。同时提供理论保证：最坏情况下不显著劣于标准BO，偏好与目标一致时收敛更快。

Result: 在物理、化学、生物学、材料科学等干实验基准上一致优于现有方法。在Fe-Cr电池电解液湿实验中，LGBO在6次迭代内达到最佳观测值的90%，而标准BO和现有LLM增强基线需要10次以上。

Conclusion: LGBO为将LLM集成到科学优化流程提供了有前景的方向，实现了语义推理与数值优化的有效结合。

Abstract: Scientific discovery is increasingly constrained by costly experiments and limited resources, underscoring the need for efficient optimization in AI for science. Bayesian Optimization (BO), though widely adopted for balancing exploration and exploitation, often exhibits slow cold-start performance and poor scalability in high-dimensional settings, limiting its applicability in real-world scientific problems. To overcome these challenges, we propose LLM-Guided Bayesian Optimization (LGBO), the first LLM preference-guided BO framework that continuously integrates the semantic reasoning of large language models (LLMs) into the optimization loop. Unlike prior works that use LLMs only for warm-start initialization or candidate generation, LGBO introduces a region-lifted preference mechanism that embeds LLM-driven preferences into every iteration, shifting the surrogate mean in a stable and controllable way. Theoretically, we prove that LGBO does not perform significantly worse than standard BO in the worst case, while achieving significantly faster convergence when preferences align with the objective. Empirically, LGBO consistently outperforms existing methods across diverse dry benchmarks in physics, chemistry, biology, and materials science. Most notably, in a new wet-lab optimization of Fe-Cr battery electrolytes, LGBO attains \textbf{90\% of the best observed value within 6 iterations}, whereas standard BO and existing LLM-augmented baselines require more than 10. Together, these results suggest that LGBO offers a promising direction for integrating LLMs into scientific optimization workflows.

</details>

Abstract: Optimization models developed by operations research (OR) experts are often deployed as decision-support systems in industrial settings. This paper introduces an agentic re-optimization framework in which a large language model (LLM) acts as an OR expert, dynamically supporting end users through natural-language interaction. The LLM translates user prompts into structured updates of the underlying optimization model, selects suitable re-optimization techniques from an optimization toolbox, and solves the resulting instance to return implementable solutions. The toolbox leverages primal information, including historical solutions, valid inequalities, solver configurations, and metaheuristics, to accelerate re-optimization while preserving solution quality. The proposed framework enables interactive and continuous adaptation of deployed optimization models, reducing dependence on OR experts and improving the sustainability of decision-support systems. Extensive experiments on two complementary large-scale real-world case studies demonstrate the effectiveness and scalability of the proposed framework. The first considers online supply chain re-optimization, where solutions must be generated rapidly while remaining close to the deployed plan, whereas the second focuses on offline university exam scheduling, where solution quality is prioritized over runtime. Results show that the toolbox-driven architecture significantly improves computational efficiency through primal-based and solver-aware re-optimization techniques, while the structured patch-based updates improve interpretability and traceability of model modifications.

### [273] [Recall Isn't Enough: Bounding Commitments in Personalized Language Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16712)
*Rui Tang,Yichi Zhang,Xi Chen,Chen Dong,Youwei Yang,Yumeng Shen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Contract-Bounded Evidence Activation (CBEA)与Lexicographic Commitment Validation (LCV)方法，通过有界证据激活和结构化承诺验证，在360个测试用例中实现零失败（可用性0.49-0.60），相比基线方法（可用性0.003-0.092）大幅提升，但代价是召回率仅为0.012（基线0.53），体现了显式承诺控制与通用记忆能力之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文和记忆系统将个性化简单视为回忆问题，实际应用中系统在提交阶段常出现失败：将噪声提示转为硬约束、丢弃罕见证据、遗忘下游义务或无法处理不可行请求。作者旨在解决这些承诺提交阶段的系统故障问题。

Method: 提出CBEA（基于契约约束的证据激活）与LCV（词典序承诺验证）框架。CBEA通过类型覆盖、尾部证人机制和后果债务激活有界证据集；LCV在生成文本前验证结构化承诺，将不可行状态导向修复、弃权或重新约定。

Result: 在360个测试用例和三种生成后端上，CBEA+LCV在验证器范围内达到零失败，可用性为0.49-0.60。使用相同LCV栅门的原始基线和长上下文基线仅达到0.003-0.092可用性。CBEA+LCV对未编译可见事实的召回率为0.012，而基线为0.53。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了一个有界运行点：显式承诺控制，中位输入payload降低74-75%，但并非追求通用记忆优势。这是一种在承诺可靠性与记忆覆盖率之间的权衡设计。

Abstract: Long-context and memory systems usually treat personalization as a recall problem. In practice, many failures occur later, when a system commits: it turns noisy hints into hard constraints, drops rare witnesses, forgets downstream obligations, or answers despite infeasibility. We introduce Contract-Bounded Evidence Activation (CBEA) with Lexicographic Commitment Validation (LCV). CBEA activates a bounded evidence set using typed coverage, tail witnesses, and consequence debt; LCV validates structured commitments before prose and routes infeasible states to repair, abstention, or recontract. Across 360 fixtures and three generation backends, CBEA+LCV reaches zero failures within validator scope at 0.49-0.60 availability over attempted runs. Raw and long-context baselines with the same LCV gate reach zero only at 0.003-0.092. A shadow oracle diagnostic marks the limit: CBEA+LCV recalls 0.012 of uncompiled visible facts, while raw recalls 0.53. The result is a bounded operating point: explicit commitment control and 74-75% lower median input payload, not universal memory dominance.

We advance this agenda along four axes: establishing $\textit{why}$ such provenance is a structural necessity by identifying responsibility gaps across sociotechnical dimensions, formalizing $\textit{what}$ it must encode through a causal attribution function and responsibility tensor, discussing $\textit{how}$ it can be made computable across four lifecycle layers with preliminary experiments showing that provenance is estimable and interveneable online before irreversible harm accumulates, and examining $\textit{who}$ bears responsibility through a concrete agentic incident. We propose CyberCorrect, a framework that formalizes LLM self-correction as a closed-loop control system grounded in cybernetic theory. The framework models the LLM generator as the plant and introduces a tri-modal Error Detector (combining self-consistency, verbalized confidence, and logic-chain verification) as the sensor. A type-directed Correction Controller generates targeted repair instructions based on diagnosed error categories, while a Convergence Judge determines iteration termination using stability criteria adapted from control theory. We further introduce three control-theoretic evaluation metrics -- convergence rate, overshoot rate, and oscillation rate -- that capture correction dynamics beyond final accuracy. Experiments on our constructed CyberCorrect-Bench (440 reasoning tasks with annotated error types and correction paths) show that CyberCorrect achieves 79.8% final accuracy, improving upon the best existing self-correction method by 6.2 percentage points, while reducing overshoot (erroneous over-correction) by 41% through its convergence control mechanism.

To address this, we propose HyperPersona, a framework that explicitly models the hierarchical organization of text (document, sentence, and word) through hypergraph structure, where a document and its sentences are represented as hyperedges, and the words are represented as nodes, enabling joint modeling of global, local, and lexical dependencies of text. Followed by a transformer-based graph encoder that learns interactions within and across these linguistic layers, yielding context-sensitive and structurally grounded feature representations for personality prediction. Experiments on the Big Five personality dimensions show that, while relying solely on text, HyperPersona effectively integrates multi-level linguistic cues, achieving superior performance compared to state-of-the-art baselines. These findings underscore the critical role of textual hierarchy in advancing human-like personality inference from natural language.

Conclusion: 结构化定性判断可以在不牺牲可解释性和人类对齐的前提下实现规模化运作，QQJ可作为现代生成式AI系统可靠评估的实用基础。

Traditional automatic metrics rely on surface-level statistical similarity and often fail to reflect human perceptions of quality, while purely human evaluation, although reliable, is costly, subjective, and difficult to scale. Recent approaches using large language models as evaluators offer improved scalability but frequently lack explicit grounding in human-defined evaluation principles, leading to bias and inconsistency. In this paper, we introduce Quantifying Qualitative Judgment (QQJ), a scalable and human-centric evaluation framework that explicitly bridges the gap between human judgment and automated assessment. QQJ separates the definition of quality from its execution by anchoring evaluation in expert-designed, multi-dimensional rubrics and calibrating large language model evaluators to align with expert reasoning using a small, high-quality annotation set. This design enables consistent, interpretable, and scalable evaluation across diverse generative tasks and modalities. Extensive experiments on text and image generation demonstrate that QQJ achieves substantially stronger alignment with human judgment than traditional automatic metrics and unconstrained LLM-based evaluators. Moreover, QQJ exhibits improved stability across repeated evaluations and superior diagnostic capability in identifying critical failure modes such as hallucination and intent mismatch. These results indicate that structured qualitative judgment can be operationalized at scale without sacrificing interpretability or human alignment, positioning QQJ as a practical foundation for reliable evaluation of modern generative AI systems.

</details>

To evaluate whether the system extracts meaningful information from these EEG signals, the results are compared with a random baseline. *Ethan Tang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文训练了一个25M参数的小型字符级语言模型KinGPT，仅用（棋局，最佳走法）数据训练，就在国际象棋谜题上超越了大模型。作者指出，现有象棋语言模型的优秀表现主要来自模式匹配而非真正理解规则，并提出LLM-Modulo框架（结合外部验证器）能以更低成本显著提升大模型性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 训练KinGPT（25M参数，字符级，仅用(position, best-move)对）；2) 对多个大模型（ChessGPT, C1-4B等）进行标准puzzle评测；3) 提出LLM-Modulo框架，将通用LLM与外部验证器结合，通过迭代验证提升走法质量。

We examine several claims made in existing literature regarding chess-trained language models and assert that their impressive benchmark performance is largely explained by pattern-matching. We also demonstrate how LLM-Modulo, a verifier-in-the-loop framework, raises RedPajama 3B's best move accuracy from 1.2% to 21.2% and move generation validity from 19.3% to 95.3% on mate-in-N chess puzzles, comparable to gains achieved from ChessGPT's fine-tuning on chess-specific web corpora at a fraction of the cost. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理的记忆系统常基于语义相似性或历史记录检索上下文，将检索到的记忆视为同等有用，但事实上记忆可能主题相关却无关、过时或误导，亟需一种能区分记忆因果有用性的方法。

Method: 提出CMI（Causal Memory Intervention），一种因果记忆选择技术，通过受控干预估计候选记忆对模型答案的因果影响，选择能提升任务性能的记忆，同时抑制不稳定、不相关或有害的记忆。并构建Causal-LoCoMo基准，包含用户请求、结构化记忆库、有用记忆、无关干扰和合成有害记忆。

Result: CMI与向量、图、反思、摘要、全历史、无记忆等基线对比，在回答质量与抗误导记忆的鲁棒性之间取得更优平衡。

Conclusion: 可靠的长期记忆需要基于因果有用性而非仅相关性来选择上下文。

Abstract: Long-horizon LLM agents rely on persistent memory to support interactions across sessions, yet existing memory systems often retrieve context using semantic similarity or broad history inclusion, treating retrieved memories as uniformly useful. This assumption is fragile because memories may be topically related while remaining irrelevant, stale, or misleading. We propose Causal Memory Intervention (CMI), a causal memory-selection technique that estimates how candidate memories affect the model's answer under controlled interventions, selecting memories that improve task performance while suppressing unstable, irrelevant, or harmful ones. To evaluate this setting, we introduce Causal-LoCoMo, a causally annotated benchmark derived from long conversational data, where each example contains a user request, a structured memory bank, useful memories, irrelevant distractors, and synthetic harmful memories. We compare CMI against vector, graph, reflection, summary, full-history, and no-memory baselines. Results show that CMI achieves a stronger balance between answer quality and robustness to misleading memory, suggesting that reliable long-term memory requires selecting context based on causal usefulness rather than relevance alone. The full framework, benchmark construction code, and experimental pipeline are available at https://github.com/Saksham4796/causal-memory-intervention.

### [284] [Entropy-Gradient Inversion: Moving Toward Internal Mechanism of Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17770)
*Junyao Yang,Chen Qian,Kun Wang,Linfeng Zhang,Quanshi Zhang,Yong Liu,Dongrui Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 形式化定义熵-梯度反转（Entropy-Gradient Inversion），即token熵与logit梯度之间的稳健负相关关系；(2) 提出Correlation-Regularized Group Policy Optimization (CorR-PO)，将该反转特征作为正则化项嵌入RL奖励函数中。

Result: 在多个推理基准和多尺度模型上的实验表明，CorR-PO一致性地优于最先进的基线方法，且更强的熵-梯度反转与更优的推理性能呈正相关。

Conclusion: 熵-梯度反转是LRM推理能力的可靠几何指纹，将其作为RL正则化约束能有效提升模型推理性能，为理解LRM内部推理机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: The advancement of Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) has catalyzed a paradigm shift from reactive ``fast thinking'' text generation to systematic, step-by-step ``slow thinking'' reasoning, unlocking state-of-the-art performance in complex mathematical and logical tasks. However, the field faces \textit{the fundamental gap between token-level behavioral analysis and internal reasoning mechanisms, and the instability of reinforcement learning (RL) for reasoning optimization relying on costly external verifiers}. We identify and formally define \textbf{Entropy-Gradient Inversion}, a robust negative correlation between token entropy and logit gradients that acts as a definitive geometric fingerprint for LRM reasoning capability. Building on this, we propose \textbf{Correlation-Regularized Group Policy Optimization (CorR-PO)}, which embeds this inversion signature into RL reward regularization. Extensive experiments on various reasoning benchmarks across multiple model scales show CorR-PO consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, confirming that stronger inversion directly correlates with superior reasoning performance.

### [285] [Remembering More, Risking More: Longitudinal Safety Risks in Memory-Equipped LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17830)
*Ahmad Al-Tawaha,Shangding Gu,Peizhi Niu,Ruoxi Jia,Ming Jin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出触发-探针协议（trigger-probe protocol），在只读记忆快照上评估固定探针集，结合NullMemory反事实基线识别记忆引发的违规；在记录、备忘录、表单、邮件等三类部署场景和八种记忆架构上测试，并在OpenClaw类智能体上验证。

Conclusion: 记忆安全应被视为纵向属性（长期评估），而非单状态快照可捕捉的属性；建议将时序评估纳入智能体安全体系。

Abstract: Safety evaluations of memory-equipped LLM agents typically measure within-task safety: whether an agent completes a single scenario safely, often under adversarial conditions such as prompt injection or memory poisoning. In deployment, however, a single agent serves many independent tasks over a long horizon, and memory accumulated during earlier tasks can affect behavior on later, unrelated ones. Studying this regime requires evaluation along the temporal dimension across tasks: not whether an agent is safe at any single memory state, but how its safety profile changes as memory accumulates across many independent interactions. We call this failure mode temporal memory contamination. To isolate memory exposure from stream non-stationarity, we introduce a trigger-probe protocol that evaluates a fixed probe set against read-only memory snapshots at varying prefix lengths, together with a NullMemory counterfactual baseline for identifying memory-induced violations. We apply this protocol across three deployment scenarios spanning records, memos, forms, and email correspondence and eight memory architectures, and additionally on Claw-like AI agents, such as OpenClaw, using the platform's native memory mechanism. Memory-enabled agents consistently exceed the NullMemory baseline, and memory-induced violation rates show a robust upward trend with exposure length on both agent classes. Order-randomization experiments indicate that the effect is driven primarily by accumulated content rather than encounter order. Finally, a structural consequence of the event decomposition is that memory-induced risk is detectable from retrieval state before generation, which we confirm with a high-recall diagnostic monitor. Our results argue for treating memory safety as a longitudinal property that requires temporal evaluation, not a single-state property that can be captured by a snapshot.

### [286] [Agentic Chunking and Bayesian De-chunking of AI Generated Fuzzy Cognitive Maps: A Model of the Thucydides Trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17903)
*Akash Kumar Panda,Olaoluwa Adigun,Bart Kosko*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 使用LLM作为智能体将文本切分为重叠文本块；2) 为每个文本块生成因果FCM；3) 通过凸混合（convex mixing）合并这些块级FCM形成统一的循环因果知识图谱；4) 利用稀疏矩阵实现轻量计算；5) 应用算子级贝叶斯推理生成“去块化”后验FCM。

Abstract: We automatically generate feedback causal fuzzy cognitive maps (FCMs) from text by teaching large-language-model agents to break the text into overlapping chunks of text. Convex mixing of these chunk FCMs gives a representative cyclic FCM knowledge graph. The text chunks can have different levels of overlap. The chunk FCMs still mix to form a new FCM causal knowledge graph. The mixing technique scales because it uses light computation with sparse causal chunk matrices. The mixing structure allows an operator-level type of Bayesian inference that produces "de-chunked" or posterior-like FCMs from the mixed FCM. These de-chunked FCMs are useful in their own right and allow further iterations of Bayesian updating. We demonstrate these mixing techniques on the essay text of Allison's "Thucydides Trap" model of conflict between a dominant power such as the United States and a rising power such as China. The FCM dynamical systems predict outcomes as they equilibrate to fixed-point or limit-cycle attractors. Seven out of 8 FCM knowledge graphs predicted a type of war when we stimulated them by turning on and keeping on the concept node that stands for the rising power's ambition and entitlement. Gemini 3.1 LLMs served as the chunking AI agents.

### [287] [TRACE: Trajectory Correction from Cross-layer Evidence for Hallucination Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18163)
*Tej Sanibh Ranade*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出TRACE算法，通过分析LLM内部跨层证据轨迹，在推理时动态选择最佳的修正层和修正操作来消除幻觉，无需训练或外部知识，在15个模型上均取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉修正方法存在结构性缺陷：它们假设幻觉修正是一个单向过程，要么固定对比某两层、要么沿单一方向干预，忽略了跨层事实证据的非均匀演化——有些错误是内部正确证据被后续层抑制，有些则是多种候选始终竞争。缺乏一种能根据具体情况自适应选择修正策略的通用方法。

Method: TRACE是一种确定性、无需训练的推理时算法，通过分析LLM前向传播中每个输入的跨层候选轨迹，动态决定：(1) 应该修正哪个层；(2) 使用哪种修正算子（标量反转、早期状态恢复、候选空间修正）。所有决策仅依赖模型内部证据，无需标签、检索、预训练或微调。

Result: 在15个模型、8个模型家族、3个事实性基准上，TRACE在所有评估单元均取得提升，平均+12.26 MC1分和+8.65 MC2-style分，最高可达+47.20 MC1和+43.38 MC2-style分，且无任何退化案例。

Conclusion: 幻觉修正不应是单一固定的干预形式。TRACE证明了自适应、多模式的跨层证据修正策略是通用且有效的，标志着从"固定干预"向"动态诊断-修正"范式的转变。

Abstract: Hallucination correction is not a one-direction problem. We show that intermediate layers are neither uniformly more truthful than final layers nor uniformly less trustworthy. Yet hallucination reduction is usually instantiated through one fixed intervention form: contrast one layer against another, steer along a truthfulness direction, or defer to external evidence. This framing is structurally incomplete. Cross-layer factual evidence does not evolve uniformly: in some failures truthful support is present internally and later suppressed, whereas in others candidate competition remains genuinely multi-directional across depth, so no single signed scalar family is generally sufficient. We introduce Trajectory Correction from Cross-layer Evidence for Hallucination Reduction (TRACE), a deterministic, training-free algorithm which corrects hallucinations at inference time by deriving both the corrective layer and the appropriate correction operator from each input's cross-layer candidate trajectory inside the LLM's own forward pass. Under one frozen hyperparameter setting, TRACE selects among scalar reversal, earlier-state recovery, and candidate-space correction using only model-internal evidence. Evaluated as a single universal algorithm across 15 models, 8 model families, and 3 factuality benchmarks, TRACE improves every evaluation cell, yielding mean gains of +12.26 MC1 points and +8.65 MC2-style points with no regressions, with gains reaching +47.20 MC1 and +43.38 MC2-style points. The method uses no labels, retrieval, pretraining, finetuning, or per-model calibration.

</details>


### [288] [Scalable Environments Drive Generalizable Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18181)
*Jiayi Zhang,Fanqi Kong,Guibin Zhang,Maojia Song,Zhaoyang Yu,Jianhao Ruan,Jinyu Xiang,Bang Liu,Chenglin Wu,Yuyu Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文主张，要实现智能体的泛化能力，关键不在于增加任务数量或交互轨迹，而在于**环境扩展**——即让智能体接触具有不同可执行规则集的环境。文章提出了轨迹扩展、任务扩展和环境扩展的统一分类法，并讨论了可扩展环境的构建范式（程序化生成器 vs 生成式世界模型），以及如何将环境扩展与状态化学习机制结合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体在训练分布外的任务和未见过环境中泛化能力差，现有扩展实践（增加轨迹或任务集）忽视了底层规则集的变化，导致智能体在接口、动态、观测或反馈信号改变时表现脆弱。核心挑战是**世界级分布偏移**，需要系统性地让智能体接触具有不同可执行规则集的环境。

Method: 1. 提出统一分类法，区分轨迹扩展（trajectory scaling）、任务扩展（task scaling）和环境扩展（environment scaling）；2. 综合两种环境构建范式：程序化生成器（强调可控性和可验证性）与生成式世界模型（强调覆盖范围和开放性）；3. 提出环境扩展可与状态化学习机制（特别是学到的更新规则）耦合，实现跨环境适应。

Result: 论文本身是立场论文（position paper），未提出具体实验结果，而是提供了概念框架和分类体系，论证环境扩展是通往鲁棒通用智能体的必要基础。

Conclusion: 可扩展环境为衡量和可控地推进鲁棒通用智能体提供了必不可少的基质（substrate）。论文呼吁研究界从单纯扩展任务和轨迹转向系统性地扩展环境规则集。

Abstract: Generalizable agents should adapt to diverse tasks and unseen environments beyond their training distribution. This position paper argues that such generalization requires environment scaling: expanding the distribution of executable rule-sets that agents interact with, rather than only increasing trajectories or tasks within fixed benchmarks. Current scaling practices largely focus on collecting more experience or broader task sets under fixed interaction rules, leaving agents brittle when underlying interfaces, dynamics, observations, or feedback signals change. The core challenge is therefore a world-level distribution shift: agents need systematic exposure to environments with meaningfully different executable rule-sets. To clarify this challenge, we propose a unified taxonomy that separates trajectory scaling, task scaling, and environment scaling by their primary deliverables and by what changes in the executable rule-set. Building on this taxonomy, we synthesize construction paradigms for scalable environments, contrasting programmatic generators that prioritize controllability and verifiability with generative world models that offer broader coverage and open-endedness. We further outline how environment scaling can be coupled with stateful learning mechanisms, emphasizing learned update rules for cross-environment adaptation. We conclude by discussing alternative perspectives and argue that scalable environments provide the essential substrate for measurable and controllable progress toward robust general agents.

</details>


### [289] [SD-Search: On-Policy Hindsight Self-Distillation for Search-Augmented Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18299)
*Yufei Ma,Zihan Liang,Ben Chen,Zhipeng Qian,Huangyu Dai,Lingtao Mao,Xuxin Zhang,Chenyi Lei,Wenwu Ou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SD-Search通过on-policy hindsight self-distillation，让策略自身产生步骤级监督信号，无需外部教师模型或额外标注，在GRPO粗粒度轨迹奖励之上叠加密集的查询级信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 搜索增强推理Agent在强化学习中使用结果奖励时，每个搜索决策共享相同的轨迹级奖励，缺乏对单个查询的步骤级信用分配。现有过程监督方法依赖更大的教师模型或外部系统生成的子问题标注，成本高昂。

Method: 单个模型扮演两个角色：学生（仅见推理时上下文）和教师（额外条件于hindsight block，包含同一问题多个rollout的查询和结果）。教师知晓哪些决策成功，学生通过最小化查询位置的token级Jensen-Shannon散度来模仿教师行为，在GRPO的粗粒度奖励上叠加密集步骤级信号。

Result: 该方法通过策略自身在标准RL训练循环内产生步骤级信号，无需外部模型推理、辅助标注流水线或额外训练阶段。

Conclusion: SD-Search提供了一种自包含的步骤级信用分配方案，在不引入外部资源的前提下提升搜索增强推理Agent的强化学习效率。

Abstract: Search-augmented reasoning agents interleave internal reasoning with calls to an external retriever, and their performance relies on the quality of each issued query. However, under outcome-reward reinforcement learning, every search decision in a rollout shares the same trajectory-level reward, leaving individual queries without step-specific credit. Recent process-supervision approaches address this gap by drawing step-level signals from outside the policy, relying either on a much larger teacher model, or on sub-question annotations produced by a stronger external system. In contrast, we propose SD-Search, which derives step-level supervision from the policy itself through on-policy hindsight self-distillation, requiring neither an external teacher nor additional annotations. In SD-Search, a single model plays two roles that differ only in conditioning: a student that sees only the context available at inference time, and a teacher that additionally conditions on a compact hindsight block summarizing the search queries and final outcomes of a group of rollouts sampled from the same question. Since the teacher knows how each rollout unfolded and which ones succeeded, its query distribution implicitly marks which decisions were worth making, and the student is trained to recover this behavior by minimizing the token-level Jensen--Shannon divergence to the teacher at search-query positions. This layers a dense, step-level signal on top of GRPO's coarse trajectory reward. Crucially, this signal is produced by the policy itself within the standard RL training loop, without external model inference, auxiliary annotation pipeline, or additional training stage.

</details>


### [290] [GIM: Evaluating models via tasks that integrate multiple cognitive domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18663)
*Rohit Patel,Alexandre Rezende,Steven McClain*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出GIM基准测试：820道原创问题，通过整合多种认知操作（而非依赖专业知识）增加难度，并利用IRT模型校准，对22个模型、47种测试配置进行系统评估，发现同系列模型的配置选择（如思考预算、量化）与模型选择同等重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM基准测试存在两种极端：一是依赖专业知识（混淆记忆与能力），二是完全脱离实际上下文进行抽象推理。作者希望设计一种既不依赖专业门槛、又能保持推理任务真实性的基准。

Method: 构建GIM基准：820道专家原创问题（615公开+205私有），每道题需协调多种认知操作（约束满足、状态追踪、认识警觉、受众校准）；采用rubric分解评分（中位数6个独立评判标准）；平衡公开/私有划分用于污染诊断；使用连续响应2PL IRT模型校准（>20万提示-响应对），产出稳健的能力估计。

Result: 对22个模型、47种测试配置（模型+思考级别的组合）进行全面排行榜；对11个模型进行35种测试配置的测试时计算-模型能力权衡研究，发现同系列配置（思考预算、量化）的影响与模型选择相当。

Conclusion: GIM通过"整合"而非"知识"或"纯粹抽象"来增加难度，提供了更贴近实际推理能力的评估方式；测试时计算配置的优化应被视为与模型选择同等重要的维度。

Abstract: As LLM benchmarks saturate, the evaluation community has pursued two strategies to increase difficulty: escalating knowledge demands (GPQA, HLE) or removing knowledge entirely in favor of abstract reasoning (ARC-AGI). The first conflates memorization with capability; the second divorces reasoning from the practical contexts in which it matters. We take a different approach. The Grounded Integration Measure (GIM) is a benchmark of 820 original problems (615 public, 205 private) where difficulty comes from integration; individual problems require coordinating multiple cognitive operations (constraint satisfaction, state tracking, epistemic vigilance, audience calibration) over broadly accessible knowledge, so that reasoning stays grounded in realistic tasks without being gated on specialized expertise. Each problem is an original expert-authored composition, majority with rubric-decomposed scoring (median 6 independently judged criteria). A balanced public--private split provides built-in contamination diagnostic. We calibrate a continuous response 2-parameter logistic (2PL) IRT model over >200k prompt-response pairs across 28 models, producing robust ability estimates that correctly order test-configurations even when raw accuracy is distorted by errors or missing data, addressing a common challenge in benchmark reporting. Using this framework, we present a comprehensive leaderboard spanning 22 models and 47 test-configurations (unique model, thinking-level pairs), and conduct what is to our knowledge the most extensive published study of how test-time compute trades off against model capability on a fixed benchmark: 11 models swept across 35 test-configurations. We observe that within-family configuration choices, such as thinking budget and quantization, matter as much as model selection. We release the evaluation framework, calibrated IRT parameters, and all public problems.

</details>

### [292] [A Hybrid Gaussian Process Regression Framework for Stable Volatility-Covariance Estimation: Evidence from Global Equity Indices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17275)
*Ujjwala Vadrevu*

Main category: q-fin.RM

TL;DR: 提出了一种混合高斯过程回归-历史模拟（GPR-HS）框架，通过解耦波动率-协方差矩阵估计，结合Matern 5/2核的动态单变量GPR与历史协方差，并引入激进噪声初始化（ANI）策略，在七只全球股指组合上实现了优于传统模型的VaR和ES预测，尤其在ES上达到100%通过率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统计量模型（GARCH族、EWMA等）存在参数刚性、分布假设严格、压力下数值不稳定等问题，导致尾部风险系统性低估，难以满足ICAAP和CCAR等监管资本充足要求。

Method: 将VCV估计解耦为两部分：①单个资产波动率用带Matern 5/2核的单变量GPR动态建模；②资产间相关性用稳定的历史协方差估计。关键创新是ANI策略——将初始白噪声核方差设为训练收益的经验方差，确保Gram矩阵正定、正则化，产生保守且合规的预测。采用滚动窗口前链交叉验证（2020.06-2025.06）评估。

Result: GPR-HS框架在大多数测试分裂中满足监管要求；投资组合层面ES通过率100%；单变量层面，按二次损失衡量71.4%的案例优于静态历史VaR基准，按违规次数衡量100%优于基准。

Conclusion: 所提出的GPR-HS框架结合ANI策略，能够在保持正则化的同时产生监管合规的保守预测，有效克服传统模型在尾部风险估计上的不足。

Abstract: Accurate forecasting of the Volatility-Covariance Matrix (VCV) is central to regulatory capital adequacy processes such as the Internal Capital Adequacy Assessment Process (ICAAP) and the Comprehensive Capital Analysis and Review (CCAR). Traditional econometric models, including GARCH-family and Exponentially Weighted Moving Average (EWMA) approaches, suffer from parametric rigidity, distributional assumptions, and numerical instability under stress, leading to systematic underestimation of tail risk. This paper proposes and validates a novel Hybrid Gaussian Process Regression-Historical Simulation (GPR-HS) framework for estimating Value-at-Risk (VaR) and Expected Shortfall (ES) across a diversified portfolio of seven major global equity indices. The framework decouples the VCV estimation problem: individual asset volatilities are modelled dynamically using Univariate GPR with a Matern 5/2 kernel, while inter-asset correlations are estimated via stable historical covariance. A key methodological contribution is the Aggressive Noise Initialization (ANI) strategy, which sets the initial White Noise kernel variance equal to the empirical variance of the training returns, ensuring Gram matrix positive-definiteness, regularization, and conservative, regulatory-compliant forecasts. Evaluated using an expanding window forward-chaining cross-validation scheme over June 2020 -June 2025, the GPR-HS framework achieves regulatory compliance in the majority of test splits; including a 100% ES pass rate at the portfolio level, while outperforming the static Historical VaR benchmark in 71.4% of univariate cases by Quadratic Loss and 100% of cases by violation count.

</details>


### [293] [Mortality Heterogeneity and Actuarial Fairness in China's Notional Defined Contribution Pension System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17768)
*Xiaoyu Dong,Hong Li,Kenneth Q. Zhou,Xiaobai Zhu*

Main category: q-fin.RM

TL;DR: 本文研究中国名义账户制养老金体系中，因收入群体死亡率差异导致的精算不公平问题。通过构建死亡率分化的Lee-Carter模型，结合1994-2020年全国死亡数据与CHARLS子群体数据（2011-2020），发现当前仅依赖退休年龄的官方年金除数导致显著的逆向再分配——高收入群体补贴低收入群体。论文提出四种收入依赖的年金化规则，能有效减少逆向转移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中国名义账户制养老金体系当前采用仅基于退休年龄的统一年金除数，未考虑不同收入群体的死亡率差异。由于高收入群体通常寿命更长，这种单一除数导致低收入群体（寿命较短）补贴高收入群体，产生精算不公平和逆向再分配问题。本文旨在量化这一不公平程度，并提出改进方案。

Method: 构建死亡率分化的Lee-Carter模型，包含群体特定的基线死亡率表和共同的时期效应；通过Hermite样条参数化基线死亡率以在数据有限条件下实现简洁建模；结合1994-2020年全国死亡率数据与CHARLS 2011-2020年子群体数据进行估计。

Result: 当前仅基于年龄的年金除数导致显著的精算不公平：补贴随收入单调递增，既产生总体精算赤字，又造成从低收入退休者向高收入退休者的逆向转移。提出的四种收入依赖的年金化规则（从简单分档设计到边际规则替代方案）均能大幅减少逆向转移。

Conclusion: 中国名义账户制养老金体系需要引入收入依赖的年金化规则以消除因死亡率差异导致的精算不公平和逆向再分配，所提出的四种方案均能有效改善现状。

Abstract: We study actuarial fairness in China's notional defined contribution (NDC) pension system when mortality differs across income groups. Under current rules, individual account balances are converted into monthly benefits using an official annuity divisor that depends only on retirement age. We develop a mortality-differentiated Lee-Carter framework with group-specific baseline mortality schedules and a common period effect, estimated by combining national mortality data for 1994-2020 with CHARLS subgroup data for 2011-2020. To model cross-group mortality parsimoniously under limited data, we parameterize the baseline schedules using Hermite splines. Applying the model to China's NDC system, we find substantial actuarial unfairness in the current age-only divisor. The subsidy rises monotonically with income, implying both an aggregate actuarial shortfall and a reverse transfer from poorer to richer retirees. We then compare four implementable income-dependent annuitization rules, ranging from a simple bracket design to marginal-rule alternatives, and show that all substantially reduce the reverse transfer.

### [294] [Asymptotic Behaviour of Unexpected Losses and Risk Ratios for Co-Monotonic Alternatives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18049)
*Max Nendel*

Main category: q-fin.RM

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型信用和保险投资组合中，非线性损失估值与均值之间的"意外损失"渐近行为。主要发现：对于单调现金可加风险度量，满足弱大数定律的一致可积性条件等价于原点处的标量连续性；对于正齐次风险度量，意外损失为o(n̄λ_n)阶；建立了Choquet保险保费类似结果，并推导了风险比率极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大型加权投资组合中超出均值的"意外损失"（即监管资本缓冲或风险边际）的渐近行为，为银行和保险监管中风险度量的合理性提供理论依据。

Method: 基于Banach格值Orlicz空间上的单调现金可加风险度量，利用弱大数定律和一致可积性条件，建立收敛性与标量连续性的等价关系，并推导渐近阶数。

Result: 1) 满足弱大数定律的一致可积性等价于原点处标量连续性；2) 正齐次风险度量下意外损失为o(n̄λ_n)；3) 建立了Choquet保险保费类似结果；4) 推导了与共单调组合比较的风险比率极限。

Conclusion: 大型投资组合中，风险度量在原点处的连续性条件决定了意外损失的收敛行为，为正齐次风险度量提供了明确的渐近阶估计，揭示了分散化带来的风险低估程度。

Abstract: The aggregation of individual risks in large credit and insurance portfolios is guided by diversification and the law of large numbers, which formalizes the convergence of sample averages to their means. At the same time, regulatory capital requirements and insurance premia are designed to provide a capital buffer or risk margin above the mean. The resulting excess, given by the difference between the nonlinear valuation of the aggregate loss and the corresponding mean, reflects the idea of protection against unexpected losses in the sense of banking and insurance regulation. This paper studies the asymptotic behaviour of this excess for large weighted portfolios. The main result shows that, for monotone cash-additive risk measures on Banach-lattice-valued Orlicz spaces, convergence along weighted averages satisfying a weak law of large numbers together with a uniform integrability condition is equivalent to scalar continuity at the origin. If the risk measure is positively homogeneous, this continuity condition is automatically satisfied, and we prove that the unexpected losses of large weighted portfolios are of order $o(n\overlineλ_n)$, where $\overlineλ_n$ denotes the average weight assigned to the first $n$ random variables. We establish analogous asymptotic results for Choquet insurance premia. Finally, we derive risk-ratio limits that quantify the potential underestimation arising when diversified portfolios are compared with co-monotonic alternatives.

### [295] [Geometric Observables for Financial Regime Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17117)
*Will Hammond*

Main category: q-fin.ST

TL;DR: 本文从学习到的权益指数收益谱嵌入中提取四种几何可观测变量（Berry相位率、谱熵、约化态纯度、哈密顿量敏感性），并将其作为体制转换检测器，在2000-2024年间17次历史危机中与46种经典和机器学习基线方法进行了比较。Berry相位率在样本外中位Cohen's d=0.72，每年假警报比随机森林少约67%。分数构建是无监督的，仅有超参数选择是有监督步骤。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Berry相位率在样本外中位Cohen's d=0.72（95%置信区间[0.34,1.18]），每年仅1.2次假警报，远低于随机森林的3.6次。约化态纯度在样本内分离度最高（d=0.83），与吸收比率（d=0.80）接近。几何通道与经典通道相关性低（平均|ρ|≈0.22），表明它们捕捉了不同的风险信号。

Conclusion: 几何可观测变量（特别是Berry相位率）作为无监督体制转换检测器效果显著，假警报率远低于有监督方法，且与经典方法互补，为金融风险监测提供了新视角。

Abstract: We extract four geometric observables -- Berry Phase Rate, Spectral Entropy, Reduced State Purity, and Hamiltonian Sensitivity -- from a learned spectral embedding of equity-index returns and evaluate them as regime-shift detectors against 46 classical and machine-learning baselines on 17 historical crises spanning 2000-2024. Under walk-forward nested hyperparameter selection on nine labelled windows, the Berry Phase Rate achieves an unbiased out-of-sample median Cohen's $d = 0.72$ (95% percentile-bootstrap CI $[0.34, 1.18]$, 10,000 resamples) and produces approximately 67% fewer false alarms per year than a label-supervised Random Forest (1.2 vs. 3.6 per year). Reduced State Purity attains the highest in-sample separability of any method ($d = 0.83$), tied closely by the Absorption Ratio ($d = 0.80$); geometric and classical channels are largely uncorrelated (mean $|ρ| \approx 0.22$), suggesting they capture distinct risk signals. Score construction is unsupervised; hyperparameter selection is the only supervised step.

### [296] [Sequential Structure in Intraday Futures Data: LSTM vs Gradient Boosting on MNQ](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17724)
*Mathias Mesfin*

Main category: q-fin.TR

TL;DR: 本文对比了梯度提升和LSTM在微型纳斯达克100期货（MNQ）日内方向预测上的表现。使用944个交易日的5分钟OHLCV数据，四种模型配置在严格的滚动窗口验证下均未产生统计显著的样本外预测能力（最高50.89% vs 基线51.8%）。结果表明，单一品种四年的5分钟数据不足以支持可靠的序列化机器学习日内预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受基于Kronos架构等基础模型在金融K线数据上研究的启发，本文旨在检验5分钟OHLCV柱状序列在单一品种数据集尺度上是否包含可被利用的序列预测结构。

Method: 采用四种模型配置（梯度提升变体+LSTM），使用944个交易日（2021-2025）的5分钟OHLCV数据，通过严格的扩展窗口滚动向前验证，在三个样本外周期进行测试。目标变量为当日收盘价是否超过上午10:30开盘价10个点以上。

Result: 所有模型均未达到统计显著的样本外准确率：梯度提升变体组合准确率50.00%-50.89%，LSTM为50.59%。置换检验p值最高为0.135（最佳梯度提升模型）和0.515（LSTM）。特征重要性在滚动窗口间不稳定，表明拟合噪声而非稳定信号。

Conclusion: 单一品种四年的5分钟OHLCV数据不足以支撑可靠的序列机器学习日内预测。本文主要贡献在于提供了Kronos启发架构在受限真实数据集上的实证评估，为序列金融ML所需数据规模设定了经验下界。

Abstract: This paper compares gradient boosting and long short-term memory (LSTM) architectures for intraday directional prediction in Micro E-Mini Nasdaq 100 futures (MNQ). Motivated by recent foundation-model research on financial candlestick data, including the Kronos architecture, we test whether five-minute OHLCV bar sequences contain exploitable sequential predictive structure at the scale of a single instrument dataset. Using 944 trading days from 2021-2025, four model configurations are evaluated under strict expanding-window walk-forward validation across three out-of-sample periods. The target variable is whether the session close exceeds the 10:30 AM open by more than ten points. No configuration produces statistically significant out-of-sample accuracy above the 51.8% base rate. Combined OOS accuracies range from 50.00% to 50.89% across gradient boosting variants, while the LSTM achieves 50.59%. Permutation tests yield p-values of 0.135 for the best gradient boosting model and 0.515 for the LSTM, indicating no statistically significant predictive edge. Feature importance instability across walk-forward folds suggests noise fitting rather than stable structural signal capture. The results indicate that four years of single-instrument five-minute OHLCV data are insufficient for reliable sequential ML-based intraday forecasting. The primary contribution is a documented evaluation of a Kronos-inspired architecture on a constrained real-world dataset, providing an empirical lower bound on data scale requirements for sequential financial ML.

</details>

### [297] [AI Slop or AI-enhancement? Student perceptions of AI-generated media for an English for Academic Purposes course](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16275)
*David James Woo,Deliang Wang,Kai Guo*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了教师引导的AI检索增强生成（RAG）工具在EAP课程中生成补充教学材料的效果，发现学生对此类多媒体材料（尤其是视频和信息图）评价较高，偏好与学业成绩正相关，但认知负荷过重会负面影响成绩，低分学生将其用作补救支架。研究表明，合理设计的AI生成内容可成为有意义的教学工具，而非低质量"AI垃圾"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前AI-RAG工具能让教育者大规模将课程材料转化为多媒体内容，但学术界尚不清楚这类AI生成内容究竟是有效的教学支架，还是"AI slop"（高产量、低质量的垃圾内容）。作者希望厘清这一问题，验证AI生成材料在英语学术用途课程中的实际教学价值。

Method: 在香港社区学院的EAP课程中，106名英语外语学习者参与实验。教师使用Google Notebook LM等工具从课程材料和作业中生成视频、播客、信息图及个性化反馈报告。采用解释性序贯混合方法设计：问卷调查、半结构化访谈、与学术成绩的相关性分析。理论框架为技术接受模型（TAM）和认知负荷理论（CLT）。

Result: 学生对AI生成材料在感知有用性和易用性上评分较高，偏好与评估相关、以视觉和多媒体格式（特别是视频和信息图）呈现的内容。视频偏好与学业成绩正相关；但更高的认知负荷与课程成绩负相关，说明材料复杂度需谨慎控制。低分学生自发将其用作补救性学习支架。

Conclusion: RAG工具能够实现传统方法难以规模化完成的个性化反馈。当AI生成内容与学生目标及认知原则相匹配时，教师引导的AI生成可以有意义地增强EAP学习生态系统，而不会沦为AI slop。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) tools now enable educators to transform course materials into diverse multimedia at scale. However, it remains unclear whether such AI-generated content functions as a pedagogical scaffold or AI slop: high volume, low quality material. This innovative practice paper reports on the development, implementation, and evaluation of teacher-prompted, AI-generated supplemental materials in an English for Academic Purposes (EAP) course at a Hong Kong Community College. Using primarily Google Notebook LM, the instructor generated videos, podcasts, infographics, and individualized feedback reports from course materials and student work for 106 English as a Foreign Language learners. An explanatory sequential mixed-methods design comprising a survey, semi-structured interviews, and correlation analysis with academic scores was employed to examine students' preferences, perceptions, and learning outcomes. Findings are framed through the Technology Acceptance Model and Cognitive Load Theory. Students rated the materials highly for perceived usefulness and ease of use, and preferred assessment-linked content presented in visual and multimodal formats, particularly videos and infographics. Video preference correlated positively with academic performance; however, higher cognitive load was negatively associated with course grades, indicating that material complexity must be carefully calibrated. Notably, some lower-performing students independently adopted the materials as remedial scaffolds. The practice demonstrates that RAG tools enable scalable personalized feedback that would be less feasible through traditional methods. When aligned with student goals and cognitive principles, teacher-prompted AI generation can meaningfully enhance the EAP learning ecosystem rather than producing AI slop.

</details>


### [298] [Generative AI in K-12 Classrooms: A Midyear Implementation Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16277)

Result: 提供了教师使用AI的初步统计数据，但由于仅有部分学区提供行政数据，教师使用模式与学生特征之间的关联尚不完整，属于初步信号。
